guitarist.&quot;</p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Personal_life">Personal
life</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18"
title="Edit
section:
Personal
life">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Relationships_and_children">Relationships
and
children</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19"
title="Edit
section:
Relationships
and
children">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Clapton
and
<a
href="/wiki/Pattie_Boyd?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pattie
Boyd">Pattie
Boyd</a>
married
in
1979.
They
had
no
children.
In
1984
while
recording
<i>Behind
The
Sun</i>,
Clapton
began
a
relationship
with
Yvonne
Kelly,
the
manager
of
the
recording
studio
in
<a
href="/wiki/Montserrat?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Montserrat">Montserrat</a>.
Both
married
but
not
to
each
other,
the
two
had
a
daughter
in
January
1985.
She
was
named
Ruth
Kelly
Clapton,
but
her
existence
was
kept
from
the
public
until
the
media
realised
she
was
his
child
in
1991.<sup
id="cite_ref-115"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-115"><span>[</span>115<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-116"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-116"><span>[</span>116<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Clapton
and
Boyd
tried
unsuccessfully
to
have
children,
even
trying
<a
href="/wiki/In_vitro_fertilisation?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="In
vitro
fertilisation">in
vitro
fertilisation</a>
in
1984,
but
were
faced
instead
with
miscarriages.<sup
id="cite_ref-117"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-117"><span>[</span>117<span>]</span></a></sup>
They
divorced
in
1988
following
his
affair
with
Italian
model
<a
href="/wiki/Lory_Del_Santo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lory
Del
Santo">Lory
Del
Santo</a>,
who
gave
birth
to
their
son,
Conor,
on
<span
class="nowrap">21
August</span>
1986.
Conor
died
in
1991,
at
the
age
of
four
and
a
half,
when
he
fell
out
of
an
open
bedroom
window
on
the
53rd
floor
of
a
Manhattan
apartment
building.<sup
id="cite_ref-118"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-118"><span>[</span>118<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
death
of
his
son
was
the
inspiration
for
Clapton's
song,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Tears_in_Heaven?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tears
in
Heaven">Tears
in
Heaven</a>&quot;.</p>








<p>Clapton
married
Melia
McEnery
in
a
low-key
church
ceremony
in
January
2001.
Daughter
Julie
Rose
was
born
in
June
2001.
Daughter
Ella
May
was
born
in
London
in
2003.
Daughter
Sophie
Belle
was
born
in
2005.<sup
id="cite_ref-119"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-119"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup>
Grandson,
Isaac
Eric
Owen
Bartlett
born
June
2013,
by
Eric's
oldest
daughter
Ruth
and
her
husband
Dean
Bartlett.<sup
id="cite_ref-120"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-120"><span>[</span>120<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Political_views">Political
views</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20"
title="Edit
section:
Political
views">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Clapton
is
a
supporter
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Countryside_Alliance?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Countryside
Alliance">Countryside
Alliance</a>,
has
played
in
concerts
to
raise
funds
for
the
organisation
and
publicly
opposed
the
<a
href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Labour
Party
(UK)">Labour
Party</a>’s
ban
on
<a
href="/wiki/Fox_hunting?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fox
hunting">fox
hunting</a>
with
the
2004
<a
href="/wiki/Hunting_Act_2004?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hunting
Act
2004">Hunting
Act</a>.
A
spokesperson
for
Clapton
said,
&quot;Eric
supports
the
Countryside
Alliance.
He
doesn't
hunt
himself,
but
does
enjoy
rural
pursuits
such
as
fishing
and
shooting.
He
supports
the
Alliance's
pursuit
to
scrap
the
ban
on
the
basis
that
he
doesn't
agree
with
the
state's
interference
with
people's
private
pursuits.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-121"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-121"><span>[</span>121<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
2008,
he
donated
a
song
to
<a
href="/wiki/Aid_Still_Required?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aid
Still
Required">Aid
Still
Required</a>'s
CD
to
assist
with
the
restoration
of
the
devastation
done
to
Southeast
Asia
from
the
2004
tsunami.</p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Controversy_over_remarks_on_immigration">Controversy
over
remarks
on
immigration</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21"
title="Edit
section:
Controversy
over
remarks
on
immigration">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>On
5
August
1976
Clapton
provoked
an
uproar
and
lingering
controversy
when
he
spoke
out
against
<a
href="/wiki/Immigration_to_the_United_Kingdom_(1922-present_day)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Immigration
to
the
United
Kingdom
(1922-present
day)"
class="mw-redirect">increasing
immigration</a>
during
a
concert
in
<a
href="/wiki/Birmingham?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Birmingham">Birmingham</a>.
Visibly
intoxicated,
Clapton
voiced
his
support
of
controversial
political
candidate
<a
href="/wiki/Enoch_Powell?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Enoch
Powell">Enoch
Powell</a>,
and
announced
on
stage
that
Britain
was
in
danger
of
becoming
a
&quot;black
colony&quot;.
Clapton
was
quoted
as
saying,
&quot;I
think
Enoch's
right
...
we
should
send
them
all
back.
Throw
the
<a
href="/wiki/Wog?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wog">wogs</a>
out!
Keep
Britain
white!&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-122"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-122"><span>[</span>122<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
latter
phrase
was
at
the
time
a
<a
href="/wiki/British_National_Front?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="British
National
Front"
class="mw-redirect">British
National
Front</a>
slogan.<sup
id="cite_ref-123"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-123"><span>[</span>123<span>]</span></a></sup>
Clapton
continued:</p>








<blockquote>









<p>&quot;I
used
to
be
into
dope,
now
I’m
into
racism.
It’s
much
heavier,
man.
Fucking
wogs,
man.
Fucking
<a
href="/wiki/Saudi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Saudi"
class="mw-redirect">Saudis</a>
taking
over
London.
Bastard
wogs.
Britain
is
becoming
overcrowded
and
Enoch
will
stop
it
and
send
them
all
back.
The
black
wogs
and
coons
and
<a
href="/wiki/Arab?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Arab"
class="mw-redirect">Arabs</a>
and
fucking
<a
href="/wiki/Jamaican_people?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jamaican
people"
class="mw-redirect">Jamaicans</a>
and
fucking
[indecipherable]
don’t
belong
here,
we
don’t
want
them
here.
This
is
England,
this
is
a
white
country,
we
don’t
want
any
black
wogs
and
coons
living
here.
We
need
to
make
clear
to
them
they
are
not
welcome.
England
is
for
white
people,
man.
We
are
a
white
country.
I
don’t
want
fucking
wogs
living
next
to
me
with
their
standards.
This
is
Great
Britain,
a
white
country,
what
is
happening
to
us,
for
fuck's
sake?
We
need
to
vote
for
Enoch
Powell,
he’s
a
great
man,
speaking
truth.
Vote
for
Enoch,
he’s
our
man,
he’s
on
our
side,
he’ll
look
after
us.
I
want
all
of
you
here
to
vote
for
Enoch,
support
him,
he’s
on
our
side.
Enoch
for
Prime
Minister!
Throw
the
wogs
out!
Keep
Britain
white!&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-124"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-124"><span>[</span>124<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








</blockquote>








<p>This
incident,
along
with
some
controversial
remarks
made
around
the
same
time
by
<a
href="/wiki/David_Bowie?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="David
Bowie">David
Bowie</a>,
as
well
as
uses
of
<a
href="/wiki/Nazi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nazi"
class="mw-redirect">Nazi</a>-related
imagery
by
<a
href="/wiki/Sid_Vicious?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sid
Vicious">Sid
Vicious</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Siouxsie_Sioux?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Siouxsie
Sioux">Siouxsie
Sioux</a>,
were
the
main
catalysts
for
the
creation
of
<a
href="/wiki/Rock_Against_Racism?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rock
Against
Racism">Rock
Against
Racism</a>,
which
occurred
on
<span
class="nowrap">30
April</span>
1978.<sup
id="cite_ref-racism_125-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-racism-125"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
response
to
the
comments,
rock
photographer
Red
Saunders
and
others
published
an
open
letter
in
<i><a
href="/wiki/NME?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="NME">NME</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Melody_Maker?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Melody
Maker">Melody
Maker</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Sounds_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sounds
(magazine)">Sounds</a></i>,
and
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Socialist_Worker?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Socialist
Worker">Socialist
Worker</a></i>.
It
read
&quot;Come
on
Eric...
Own
up.
Half
your
music
is
black.
You're
rock
music's
biggest
colonist&quot;.
It
concluded,
&quot;P.S.
Who
shot
the
Sheriff,
Eric?
It
sure
as
hell
wasn't
you!&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-racism_125-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-racism-125"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
an
interview
from
October
1976
with
<i><a
href="/wiki/Sounds_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sounds
(magazine)">Sounds</a></i>
magazine,
Clapton
remarked,
&quot;I
thought
it
was
quite
funny
actually.
I
don't
know
much
about
politics.
I
don't
even
know
if
it
would
be
good
or
bad
for
him
to
get
in.
I
don't
even
know
who
the
Prime
Minister
is
now.
I
just
don't
know
what
came
over
me
that
night.
It
must
have
been
something
that
happened
in
the
day
but
it
came
out
in
this
garbled
thing...
I
thought
the
whole
thing
was
like
Monty
Python.
There's
this
rock
group
playing
on-stage
and
the
singer
starts
talking
about
politics.
It's
so
stupid.
Those
people
who
paid
their
money
sittin'
listening
to
this
madman
dribbling
on
and
the
band
meanwhile
getting
fidgety
thinking
'oh
dear'.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Farther_On_126-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Farther_On-126"><span>[</span>126<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
a
2004
interview
with
<i><a
href="/wiki/Uncut_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Uncut
(magazine)">Uncut</a></i>,
Clapton
referred
to
Powell
as
&quot;outrageously
brave&quot;,
and
stated
that
his
&quot;feeling
about
this
has
not
changed&quot;,
because
the
UK
is
still
&quot;...
inviting
people
in
as
cheap
labour
and
then
putting
them
in
ghettos.&quot;
In
2004
Clapton
told
an
interviewer
for
<i><a
href="/wiki/Scotland_on_Sunday?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scotland
on
Sunday">Scotland
on
Sunday</a></i>,
&quot;There's
no
way
I
could
be
a
racist.
It
would
make
no
sense&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-127"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-127"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
his
2007
autobiography,
Clapton
called
himself
&quot;deliberately
oblivious
to
it
all&quot;
and
wrote,
&quot;I
had
never
really
understood
or
been
directly
affected
by
racial
conflict
...
when
I
listened
to
music,
I
was
disinterested
in
where
the
players
came
from
or
what
colour
their
skin
was.
Interesting,
then,
that
10
years
later,
I
would
be
labelled
a
racist
...
Since
then,
I
have
learnt
to
keep
my
opinions
to
myself.
Of
course,
it
might
also
have
had
something
to
do
with
the
fact
that
Pattie
had
just
been
leered
at
by
a
member
of
the
Saudi
royal
family.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-128"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-128"><span>[</span>128<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
a
December
2007
interview
with
<a
href="/wiki/Melvyn_Bragg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Melvyn
Bragg">Melvyn
Bragg</a>
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_South_Bank_Show?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
South
Bank
Show">The
South
Bank
Show</a></i>,
Clapton
reiterated
his
support
for
Enoch
Powell
and
again
denied
that
Powell's
views
were
&quot;racist&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-129"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-129"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Wealth_and_assets">Wealth
and
assets</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22"
title="Edit
section:
Wealth
and
assets">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
2009
<i>Surrey
Life
Magazine</i>
ranked
Eric
Clapton
as
number
17
in
their
list
of
richest
<a
href="/wiki/Surrey?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Surrey">Surrey</a>
residents,
estimating
Clapton's
fortune
at
&pound;120
million
in
assets.
This
was
a
compilation
of
property
and
income
which
include
a
&pound;9
million
<a
href="/wiki/Yacht?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yacht">yacht</a>,
&quot;Va
Bene&quot;
(previously
owned
by
<a
href="/wiki/Bernie_Ecclestone?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bernie
Ecclestone">Bernie
Ecclestone</a>),
his
back
<a
href="/wiki/Music_catalog?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Music
catalog">music
catalogue</a>,
his
touring
income,
and
his
<a
href="/wiki/Marshbrook?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Marshbrook">Marshbrook</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Holding_company?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Holding
company">holding
company</a>,
which
had
earned
him
&pound;110
million
since
1989.<sup
id="cite_ref-Clapton.27s_estimated_wealth_130-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Clapton.27s_estimated_wealth-130"><span>[</span>130<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2003,
he
purchased
a
50
percent
share
of
gentleman's
outfitters
Cordings
Piccadilly.<sup
id="cite_ref-Clapton_rescues_gentlemen.27s_shop_131-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Clapton_rescues_gentlemen.27s_shop-131"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup>
At
the
time,
owner
Noll
Uloth
was
trying
to
save
the
shop
from
closure
and
thought
'I
will
go
and
talk
to
my
best
client&quot;.
He
is
reported
to
have
contacted
Clapton
and
within
five
minutes
he
had
a
reply
saying
'I
can't
let
this
happen.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Clapton_rescues_gentlemen.27s_shop_131-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Clapton_rescues_gentlemen.27s_shop-131"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Charitable_work">Charitable
work</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23"
title="Edit
section:
Charitable
work">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
1993,
Clapton
was
appointed
a
director
of
<a
href="/wiki/Clouds_House?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Clouds
House">Clouds
House</a>,
a
treatment
centre
for
drug
and
alcohol
dependence,
and
served
on
their
board
until
1997.<sup
id="cite_ref-132"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-132"><span>[</span>132<span>]</span></a></sup>
Clapton
also
served
on
the
board
of
directors
for
The
Chemical
Dependency
Centre
from
1994
until
1999.<sup
id="cite_ref-133"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-133"><span>[</span>133<span>]</span></a></sup>
Both
charities
subsequently
merged
to
become
<a
href="/wiki/Action_on_Addiction?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Action
on
Addiction">Action
on
Addiction</a>
in
2007.</p>








<p>In
1998,
he
established
the
<a
rel="nofollow"
class="external
text"
href="http://crossroadsantigua.org/">Crossroads
Center</a>
in
Antigua
to
help
others
overcome
their
addictions
to
drugs
and
alcohol
and
is
active
in
its
management
oversight
and
fundraising
to
the
present
day.<sup
id="cite_ref-134"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-134"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-135"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-135"><span>[</span>135<span>]</span></a></sup>
Clapton
has
organized
the
<a
href="/wiki/Crossroads_Guitar_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Crossroads
Guitar
Festival">Crossroads
Guitar
Festival</a>
in
2004,
2007,
2010
and
2013
to
raise
funds
for
this
center.<sup
id="cite_ref-136"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-136"><span>[</span>136<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Awards_and_honours">Awards
and
honours</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24"
title="Edit
section:
Awards
and
honours">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<table
class="wikitable"
style="width:95%;">









<tbody>









<tr>











<th
align="center">Year</th>











<th>Award
/
Recognition</th>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>1983</b></td>











<td>
<p>Presented
the
Silver
Clef
Award
from
<a
href="/wiki/Princess_Michael_of_Kent?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Princess
Michael
of
Kent">Princess
Michael
of
Kent</a>
for
outstanding
contribution
to
British
music.<sup
id="cite_ref-crossroads_137-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-crossroads-137"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>1985</b></td>











<td>
<p>Presented
with
<a
href="/wiki/BAFTA?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="BAFTA"
class="mw-redirect">BAFTA</a>
for
Best
Original
Television
Music
for
Score
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Edge_of_Darkness?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Edge
of
Darkness">Edge
of
Darkness</a></i>
with
<a
href="/wiki/Michael_Kamen?qsrc=3044"

title="Michael
Kamen">Michael
Kamen</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-138"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-138"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>1993</b></td>











<td>
<p>&quot;Tears
in
Heaven&quot;
won
three
Grammy
awards
for
Song
of
the
Year,
Record
of
the
Year,
and
Male
Pop
Vocal
Performance.
Clapton
also
won
Album
of
the
Year
and
Best
Rock
Vocal
Performance
for
<i>Unplugged</i>
and
Best
Rock
Song
for
&quot;Layla&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-139"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-139"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>1994</b></td>











<td>

the
<a
href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Order
of
the
British
Empire">OBE</a>
for
services
to
music.<sup
id="cite_ref-140"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>2000</b></td>











<td>
<p>Inducted
into
the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame
for
the
third
time,
this
time
as
a
solo
artist.
He
was
earlier
inducted
as
a
member
of
the
bands
Cream
and
The
Yardbirds.<sup
id="cite_ref-141"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>










<tr>











<td
align="center"><b>2004</b></td>











<td>

to
<a

title="CBE"
class="mw-redirect">CBE</a>,

<a

Royal</a>
at
Buckingham
Palace
as

of

Year's
Honours
list.<sup

href="#cite_note-142"><span>[</span>142<span>]</span></a></sup><sup

class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-143"><span>[</span>143<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
</td>










</tr>

<td

<td>

the
<a

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Football">Football</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25"
title="Edit
section:
Football">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>In
1982
he
performed
a
concert
before
<a
href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C.?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="West
Bromwich
Albion
F.C.">West
Bromwich
Albion</a>
player
<a
href="/wiki/John_Wile?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
Wile">John
Wile</a>'s
testimonial
game
at
<a
href="/wiki/The_Hawthorns?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Hawthorns">The
Hawthorns</a>,
and
it
is
often
reported
by
various
sources
that
Clapton
is
an
Albion
supporter.
Credence
for
this
notion
can
be
taken
from
the
cover
pictures
to
the
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Backless?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Backless">Backless</a>&quot;
solo
album,
where
he
is
seen
on
the
front
cover
to
be
wearing
a
football
scarf;
the
rear
cover
<a
rel="nofollow"
class="external
text"
href="http://www.free-covers.org/cd-covers/eric-clapton-backless-1978-cd-cover-1335.html">photograph</a>
reveals
the
slogan
&quot;ALBION&quot;
on
the
scarf.
It
has
been
reported
that
the
club
rejected
his
offer
to
invest
cash
in
the
club
around
this
time,
and
that
he
has
since
expressed
more
of
an
interest
in
<a
href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C.?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Chelsea
F.C.">Chelsea</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-145"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-145"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Clapton.27s_music_in_film_and_TV">Clapton's
music
in
film
and
TV</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Eric_Clapton&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26"
title="Edit
section:
Clapton's
music
in
film
and
TV">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Clapton's
music
has
appeared
in
dozens
of
movies
and
television
shows
as
far
back
as
1973's
<i><a
href="/wiki/Mean_Streets?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mean
Streets">Mean
Streets</a></i>
which
featured
the
song
&quot;I
Looked
Away&quot;.
Other
appearances
in
media
include
in
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Miami_Vice?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Miami
Vice">Miami
Vice</a></i>
series
(&quot;Wonderful
Tonight&quot;,
&quot;Knock
on
Wood&quot;,
&quot;She's
Waiting&quot;,
and
&quot;Layla&quot;),
<i><a
href="/wiki/Back_to_the_Future?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Back
to
the
Future">Back
to
the
Future</a></i>
(&quot;Heaven
Is
One
Step
Away&quot;),
<i><a
href="/wiki/Lethal_Weapon_2?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lethal
Weapon
2">Lethal
Weapon
2</a></i>
(&quot;Knockin'
On
Heaven's
Door&quot;),
<i><a
href="/wiki/Goodfellas?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Goodfellas">Goodfellas</a></i>
(&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Layla?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Layla">Layla</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Sunshine_of_Your_Love?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sunshine
of
Your
Love">Sunshine
of
Your
Love</a>&quot;),<sup
id="cite_ref-146"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-146"><span>[</span>146<span>]</span></a></sup>
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Friends?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Friends">Friends</a></i>
episode
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/The_One_with_the_Proposal,_Part_2?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
One
with
the
Proposal,
Part
2"
class="mw-redirect">The
One
with
the
Proposal,
Part
2</a>&quot;
(&quot;Wonderful
Tonight&quot;),
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/Men_in_Black_III?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Men
in
Black
III"
class="mw-redirect">Men
in
Black
III</a></i>
(&quot;Strange
Brew&quot;).
Also,
<a
href="/wiki/Opel?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Opel">Opel</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Vauxhall_Motors?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Vauxhall
Motors">Vauxhall</a>
used
the
guitar
riff
from
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Layla?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Layla">Layla</a>&quot;
in
their
advertising
campaigns
throughout
1987–95.
In
addition
to
his
music
appearing
in
media,
Clapton
has
contributed
to
several
movies
by
writing
or
co-writing
the
musical
scores
or
contributing
original
songs.
These
movies
include
<i><a
href="/wiki/Lethal_Weapon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lethal
Weapon">Lethal
Weapon</a></i>
(co-written
with
Michael
Kamen),
<i><a
href="/wiki/Communion_(1989_film)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Communion
(1989
film)">Communion</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Rush_(1991_film)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rush
(1991
film)">Rush</a></i>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Phenomenon_(film)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Phenomenon
(film)">Phenomenon</a></i>
(&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Change_the_World?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Change
the
World">Change
the
World</a>&quot;),
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/Lethal_Weapon_3?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lethal
Weapon
3">Lethal
Weapon
3</a></i>
(co-wrote
and
co-performed
&quot;It's
Probably
Me&quot;
with
<a
href="/wiki/Sting_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sting
(musician)">Sting</a>
and
&quot;Runaway
Train&quot;
with
Elton
John).</p>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Eric_Clapton&page=1&ac=24&qid=BEE9327473FF1920590D1E068BCA38C1&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();
